constructor(mapping(uint8 => TvmCell) code) onlyOwner {
    _position = Position({x: 0, y: 0});
    _karma = 0;
    _karma_income = 600;

    _code = code;

    // Initialize position randomly
    rnd.shuffle();
    int128 x = rnd.next(int128(61)) - int128(30);
    int128 y = rnd.next(int128(61)) - int128(30);
    _position = Position({x: x, y: y});

    _karma = 5000;
    _karma_income = 600;
    _timeupdate = block.timestamp;
}
